  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_00debca8-2d39-4af2-accc-dff9bbdc464b'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

<span id="freeTextContainer12385818472777100716">When reserved flight attendant Bianca gets one look at billionaire hotel owner James Cavendish, she loses all of her hard-won composure.   <span id="freeText12385818472777100716" style="display:none">When reserved flight attendant Bianca gets one look at billionaire hotel owner James Cavendish, she loses all of her hard-won composure. For a girl who can easily juggle a tray of champagne flutes at 35,000 feet in three inch heels, she finds herself shockingly weak-kneed from their first encounter. The normally unruffled Bianca can't seem to look away from his electrifying turquoise gaze. They hold a challenge, and a promise, that she finds impossible to resist, and she is a girl who is used to saying no and meaning it. <br /><br />Bianca is accustomed to dealing with supermodels and movie stars in her job as a first class flight attendant, but James Cavendish puts them all to shame in the looks department. If only it were just his looks that she found so irresistible about the intimidating man, Bianca could have ignored his attentions. But what tempts her like never before is the dominant pull he seems to have over her from the moment they meet, and the promise of pleasure, and pain, that she reads in his eyes.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/458462935" />
    <a title="Shelley" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7526630-shelley"><img alt="Shelley" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1370799427p2/7526630.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/458462935?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelley" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelley" href="/user/show/7526630-shelley">Shelley</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer458462935" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9216304463598009109"><b>****Contains mild spoilers and a lot of bitching* ***</b><br/><br/>I understand that there is a thriving market for the story about dominant hot young billionaires and their obsession with a beautiful insecure/traumatised young women. <br/>I also know that we are going to get some similarities here. That's fair enough. I can accept that. I even don't care too much as long as it's done right. <br/>But...COME ON! This is such a rip off! I read it wondering if the author hasn't a law suit pending.<br/><br/>Surely when deciding to c</span>
  <span id="freeText9216304463598009109" style="display:none"><b>****Contains mild spoilers and a lot of bitching* ***</b><br><br>I understand that there is a thriving market for the story about dominant hot young billionaires and their obsession with a beautiful insecure/traumatised young women. <br>I also know that we are going to get some similarities here. That's fair enough. I can accept that. I even don't care too much as long as it's done right. <br>But...COME ON! This is such a rip off! I read it wondering if the author hasn't a law suit pending.<br><br>Surely when deciding to climb on board the Fifty Shades gravy train you would have the imagination to take this in another direction and not be so darn disturbingly blatant in your efforts at reproducing what <b>is </b>ultimately another Fifty Shades. <br><br><a href="http://s1069.beta.photobucket.com/user/Paigeturner76/library/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398027ra/768760.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Allow me to make my point please. <br><br>Some things I state here might be purely coincidental. I found it hard to believe though especially when there is so much in your face, almost blatant plagiarism of the plot and characterization. <br>I read this book with my mouth hanging open. Does the author think we wouldn't notice? Jesus! <br>I read Fifty Shades more than a year ago, so this is what I can remember, just off the top of my head! <br><br> <b>Let me list a few similarities:<br><br>Billionaire in his twenties. <br><br><a href="http://s1069.beta.photobucket.com/user/Paigeturner76/media/sexy%20man%20moments/tumblr_m7luc0PHS61qaib74o1_500_zpsa6caf1a1.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398027ra/768761.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m7luc0PHS61qaib74o1_500_zpsa6caf1a1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Kinky dominant control freak.<br><br><a href="http://s1069.beta.photobucket.com/user/Paigeturner76/media/sexy%20man%20moments/560680_182783505201839_2046309791_n_zps506eece6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398027i/768762._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 560680_182783505201839_2046309791_n_zps506eece6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>The most beautiful man she's ever seen.<br><br><a href="http://s1069.beta.photobucket.com/user/Paigeturner76/media/its%20orgasmic%20and%20hot%20shew%20fans%20self/wanttositonhim_zps51c63f7d.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398027ra/768763.gif" alt=" photo wanttositonhim_zps51c63f7d.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>She turns into a simpering clumbsy idiot on their first couple of encounters.<br><br><a href="http://s1069.beta.photobucket.com/user/Paigeturner76/media/condescending%20and%20eye%20rolling/bored-eccbc87e4b5ce2fe28308fd9f2a7baf3-282.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398027ra/768764.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>He has a proposition for her.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the same kind! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and<br>he can play her body like an instrument.<br><br><a href="http://s1069.beta.photobucket.com/user/Paigeturner76/media/condescending%20and%20eye%20rolling/1790.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398027ra/768765.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>They have sex on a plane.<br><br><a href="http://s1069.beta.photobucket.com/user/Paigeturner76/media/condescending%20and%20eye%20rolling/4186.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398027ra/768766.gif" alt=" photo 4186.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>There is a playroom in his penthouse, she bites her lip and has a special best friend too! Aaaaand<br><br><a href="http://s1069.beta.photobucket.com/user/Paigeturner76/media/disbelief/4097.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398027ra/768767.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>She thinks he is way out of her league <br><br><a href="http://s1069.beta.photobucket.com/user/Paigeturner76/media/disbelief/are-you-shtting-me-eccbc87e4b5ce2fe28308fd9f2a7baf3-150.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/480159.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>He's mercurial (yep, that exact word)and he also happens to have suffered an abusive horrible childhood.<br><br>She makes a drunken mess of herself, complete with him taking her home to 'care ' for her and then sleeping together in the same bed!<br><br><a href="http://s1069.beta.photobucket.com/user/Paigeturner76/media/disbelief/tumblr_mc2j8vb6GG1r0byljo1_250.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398027ra/768768.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>There's also the proverbial blindfold along with music to shag to! <br><br><a href="http://s1069.beta.photobucket.com/user/Paigeturner76/media/hxZVg.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398027ra/768769.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>I really could go on here, but I'll save it!<br></b><br><br>Okay, so all this shocking unoriginality aside. <br><br>The MC....what's his name? <br>Oh yes. Mr Beautiful, I can't even remember his proper name. He's the 'most beautiful,' 'most stunning,' 'most attractive,' and 'most devastatingly handsome' man in the world. <br>Sadly he is also the most arrogant, conceited, hedonistic, domineering, overly possessive, mercurial (yes I'll use that word too) controlling arsehole in the whole world. <br>He is moody and sulky and way too intense, and not in a good way. I did not find him appealing or sexy at all.<br><br>It's a shame really because I'm the first one to swoon and kiss the feet of a sexy arrogant Dom. Not even when Mr beautiful shows off his sexy body, complete with the muscled V trail to heaven did I feel an ounce of admiration. <br><br>In my opinion the author pushed the lesser characteristics of a Dom a bit too far with this guy. Quite frankly, he was very disconcerting and my every instinct was screaming for the heroine to RUN! <br><br>His dialogue leaves a lot to be desired too. <br>When a man says to a virgin, who has stayed shied away from men her whole life<br><br><b>
  <i>“I'm going to tie you to the bed and take your hymen.” </i>
</b><br><br>It is not cool, or sexy or erotic. It's bloody vulgar and I would have smacked him upside the head. No matter how drunk I was.<br><br>And what about this one? Can you just for one second imagine having phone sex and the guy says this<br><br> <b><i>“Now lift up your skirt and stroke the petals of your sex lightly.”</i> </b> <br><br>Oh my freaking God! <br>Who says that? ...the petals of your sex? Is he serious...the petals of your sex?! <br> <br><br>I know a lot of people loved this and I'm not about to totally slate the entire book. I wanted to like it, I always want to love the things I read. It is rated two stars after all and if you move your mouse over the stars, two stars means it was okay. <br>So let me tell you about what saved this from being burnt.<br><br>Bianca! and Stephan. Best friends since childhood. Totally believable in the affection and caring they have for each other. Theirs is a special kind of friendship that really is something that we all covet for ourselves. Inseparable, loyal, selfless and totally devoted to each other. Together they are a winner! <br><br>Bianca is a likable enough heroine, especially because she has a spine! God I could have kissed her so many times for standing up to the arrogant SOB. I think E.L James could take a few pointers on that one. <br>Stephan gets a very big star and so does Bianca and I'm being generous because Bianca did evoke a few eye rolls from me.<br>I cannot award any more. The writing is filled with all the cheesy over used and uninspiring descriptive's that make me cringe. The sex was about erotic and sensual as a wet sock. <br><br>The finale was totally predictable <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[especially seeing as the author is following the trend. Why would I expect anything else? I didn't even list the ending in my similarities, I should have done. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I really wish I hadn't wasted my time. But hey, if you want another Fifty Shades...go for it! Or you could just do a re-read. <br><br>Okay so you can all throw stones now. I'm done saying what I needed to say. I'll go hide in the corner.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <b><br><a> Bianca Karlsson, “Bee”, “(Princess) Buttercup:</a> Swedish-American/23 years old/flight attendant-hobby artist/light blond hair/pale blue eyes/sub.</b>
</i><br><br><b>Bianca was nicknamed, (Princess) Buttercup</b> by her dear friend Stephen because she loved the movie the <b>Princess Bride</b> so much. The movie with its theme song, “Storybook Love” depicts a love so great it overcame huge obstacles, transcending time and even life as we know it. In all Bianca’s brokenness and skepticism, ultimately how could she <i>ever</i> settle for anything less?<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=aYQ4B1nuj8Y">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=aYQ4B1...</a><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“...Come my love I'll tell you a tale.<br>Of a boy and girl and their love story.<br>And how he loved her oh so much.<br>And all the charms she did possess.<br>Now this did happen once upon a time.<br>When things were not so complex.<br><b>And how he worshipped the ground she walked.<br>And when he looked in her eyes he became obsessed.</b><br>My love is like a storybook story.<br>But it's as real as the feelings I feel…”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br><u>I recommend you read the series in this order:</u><br>1. James POV 0.5: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/2013/02/guest-post-interview-giveaway-grounded.html#more">http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co....</a><br>2. In Flight, book 1, chapter 3-6 – stop!<br>5. James POV 1.2 (scroll down): <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://aestasbookblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/02/Karaoke.pdf">http://aestasbookblog.com/wp-content/...</a><br>6. James POV 1.3: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://anas-attic.com/anas_diary/up-in-the-air-series-by-rk-lilley-james-pov/">http://anas-attic.com/anas_diary/up-i...</a><br>7. In Flight, book 1, chapter 7 – stop!<br>8. James POV 1.4: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://shhmomsreading.com/exclusive-excerpt-in-flight-wake-up-call-james-pov-part-1-by-r-k-lilley/">http://shhmomsreading.com/exclusive-e...</a><br>9. In Flight, book 1, chapter 8 – stop!<br>10. James POV 1.5: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://beccathebibliophile.blogspot.com/search/label/R.K.%20Lilley">http://beccathebibliophile.blogspot.c...</a><br>11. In Flight, book 1, rest of book<br>12. Mile High, book 2, chapter 1 &amp; 2 – stop!<br>13. James POV 2.1: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jessysbookclub.wordpress.com/2013/02/08/exclusive-james-cavendish-pov-grounded-giveaway-up-in-the-air-series-by-r-k-lilley/">http://jessysbookclub.wordpress.com/2...</a><br>14. Grounded, book 3<br>15. James POV 3.1:<i>TBD</i><br><br>The moment James laid eyes on Bianca he was captivated – even obsessed. He sees a stunningly beautiful woman with so very sad pale blue eyes. The one thing Bianca has been exceptionally successful at all her life (except with her best friend Stephen) is to keep people ay a distance. Despite, or rather because of everything she has had to endure, she has protected her privacy and kept to herself. She is not interested in relationships and she is still a virgin.<br><br>James approach is so different than anything she has ever experienced. To his advantage he picks up on her submissive tendencies. He is a dom and as it turns out, for the first time in Bianca’s life, she has met a man who knows how to pursue her. That makes her curious enough to open up and let down her guard. They are so taken with other it’s electric. But they are both so broken and complex and there so much to overcome. <br><br>In this book we get to follow as James pursues Bianca relentlessly – quite a novelty for someone of James’ caliber. Needless to say book 1 ends in a cliff hanger, but no worries because book 2 and 3 are waiting. <br><br>James is everything I could ever ask for in a hero and Bianca is truly his match. This is a debut by R.K. Lilley who is an excellent storyteller. Thanks for an epic saga!<br><br><u>In book 1 we are also introduced to all the different sides of James, aka Mr. Cavendish:</u><br>Mr. Generous, Mr. Unnerving, Mr. Beautiful, Mr. Persistent, Mr. Perverse, Mr. Moody, Mr. Stalker, Mr. Angry, Mr. Kinky, Mr. Spellcaster, Mr. Dominant, Mr. BDSM, Mr. Sensitive, Mr. Insatiable, Mr. Incredible, Mr. Desperate, Mr. Possessive, Mr. Relentless, Mr. Accommodating, Mr. Bossy, Mr. Doting, Mr. Volatile, Mr. Charming, Mr. Shameless, Mr. Withdrawn, Mr. Tender-Lover, Mr. Personality, Mr. Affectionate, Mr. Gratification, Mr. Mercurial, Mr. Wonderful, Mr. Beautiful, Mr. Duplicitous, Mr. Celebrity.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“It gave me an extraordinary feeling, being on the receiving end of such a stare. It made me feel like I was more important than air to him for a brief, profound moment.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5+ stars <br>Heroine rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 5 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 5 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 5 stars<br>Story ending rating: TBA<br>***************************<br><b>Overall rating: 5 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this series: Yes.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20NIck%20Nacks/tumblr_mo8jcgQP3C1s0x7xbo1_400_zps4845075a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer18131649275064589827"><b>
  <blockquote>BE STILL MY BEATING HEART!</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>Holy Freaking <b>WOW</b>! Make room Christian Grey, Gideon Cross, Braden Carmichael – there’s a new fictional boyfriend in the harem and that man is Mr James melt my freakin' panties Cavendish. How much did I love him? Let me count the ways!<br/><br/>He’s a super uber-alpha dominant male, he’s possessive, protective, controlling, a bit of a sadist, romantic, tender, fierce, generous, caring, soulful – I could go on and on and rain down superlatives but my heart and stomach really di</span>
  <span id="freeText18131649275064589827" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>BE STILL MY BEATING HEART!</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Holy Freaking <b>WOW</b>! Make room Christian Grey, Gideon Cross, Braden Carmichael – there’s a new fictional boyfriend in the harem and that man is Mr James melt my freakin' panties Cavendish. How much did I love him? Let me count the ways!<br><br>He’s a super uber-alpha dominant male, he’s possessive, protective, controlling, a bit of a sadist, romantic, tender, fierce, generous, caring, soulful – I could go on and on and rain down superlatives but my heart and stomach really did do crazy little flip-flops the whole time I was reading this and they are still doing it now as I think back and remind myself! I have a major crush on him.<br><br><a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397708ra/767584.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>He had moved in behind me, and he gripped my hair softly, breathing warmly on my neck as he spoke. “Are you so unaffected by me?” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>He meets the very reserved flight attendant Bianca and they share an instant, mind-blowing connection. The world around them grinds to a halt as they just stare at one another, completely unable to look away. Mr Cavendish is seriously rich and uses his wealth and influence to see her again and they embark on an incredibly passionate D/s relationship.<br><br>It’s not just all about the sex though – I loved the way he tenderly took off Bianca’s make-up when she was falling down drunk, the way carried her and held her when she cried, the way he just wanted to care for her and cherish her and protect her from the world. <br><br>Of course, there’s more to it than that – they both have troubled pasts and both are keeping secrets and only a few are revealed in this instalment. One of those secrets will have huge implications for Bianca before the end of this one and they’re being so guarded that they struggle with the dynamics of their relationship.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I’m so afraid I’ll offend you beyond all repair, and that you’ll never let me know how. You’ll just leave and never speak to me again. Would you do that?”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I’d just like to give a big virtual hug to Stephan, Bianca’s best friend, a gay flight attendant, and her biggest and fiercest protector. They share a uniquely special bond and I loved him, almost as much as I loved Mr Cavendish.<br><br>Of course, there are sequels to come and this one ends with everything up in the air and on a moment of absolute desperation. There’s absolutely no way in hell that I’m not moving straight onto the sequel. I’ve given this book 5 stars. I know that I’m a generally positive reviewer, I like most of what I read but I rarely give out 5 stars but I dragged that fifth one out for this one because of how it made me feel. I just LOVED it.<br><br><a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397708i/767585.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>5 big, <b>BIG</b> STARS<br></span>

    <a title="Kala" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6551949-kala"><img alt="Kala" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1320263692p2/6551949.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer478920406" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7383004494419731699">Also posted on my blog at:<br/><a href='http://kalabookblog.blogspot.com/2012/12/in-flight-by-rk-lilley.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kala's Book Blog</a><br/><br/>This book is about as blatant of a 50Shades knockoff as you can get.<br/><br/>Bianca is a drop dead gorgeous (but she doesn't think so) flight attendant who is a 20-something year old virgin (of course) and has a traumatic past. <br/><br/>James is a billionaire who is the absolute best looking guy in the entire world (nicknamed Mr. Beautiful by Bianca).<br/><br/>Their first real meeting is on a plane while he is in first class and she's his flight attendant. He propositions her. She </span>
  <span id="freeText7383004494419731699" style="display:none">Also posted on my blog at:<br /><a href="http://kalabookblog.blogspot.com/2012/12/in-flight-by-rk-lilley.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Kala's Book Blog</a><br /><br />This book is about as blatant of a 50Shades knockoff as you can get.<br /><br />Bianca is a drop dead gorgeous (but she doesn't think so) flight attendant who is a 20-something year old virgin (of course) and has a traumatic past. <br /><br />James is a billionaire who is the absolute best looking guy in the entire world (nicknamed Mr. Beautiful by Bianca).<br /><br />Their first real meeting is on a plane while he is in first class and she's his flight attendant. He propositions her. She declines. He does it again. She declines again. Forcefully. He continues to try and proposition her. She VERY CLEARLY and VERY PURPOSEFULLY declines him AGAIN. What does he do at this point? He corners her in the galley in the plane and forces himself on her. Of course, he has magic lips and she immediately loses control and starts willingly making out with him because OMG SHE JUST CAN'T STOP IT FEELS SO GOOD.<br /><br />After he stops half raping her in the galley, she tells him again she's not interested. So what does he do? He talks her other flight attendant best friend in to telling him where Bianca will be partying that night and he shows up. James arrives at the bar and starts berating Bianca for drinking (the girl is 23 and hasn't had a drop of alcohol in 2 years). Of course she gets really drunk and her BFF roommate decides that this creepy stalker is JUST the right person to take Bianca home while he stays at the bar. (Best friend ever!)<br /><br />So James takes her home. He starts stripping her naked and she resists at first, but then because he's so super awesome she lets him get her naked. But he is a stand up guy. He tells her he is going to fuck her so hard she won't ever want another man again. But not while she is drunk! He just waits til the morning and in an really unsexy scene he grabs her boobs (and OMG IT IS SO AMAZING SHE PRACTICALLY HAS AN ORGASM RIGHT THERE!). He then gets her off with his fingers in about three seconds flat and of course, virginal Bianca feels bad for leaving him unsatisfied so she gives him a blowjob (her first time ever!). And of course, her first blow job ever, and she swallows on purpose (suuuure!).<br /><br />I'm only 17% of the way through this book and I don't think I can take it anymore. I should have stopped after the airplane scene because it was so revolting. Do you realize what he did in that plane is ILLEGAL? If I girl declines you multiple times and you force yourself on her, THAT IS A CRIME. Of course it's not in this book because "No" means "Yes" for Bianca (GREAT MESSAGE TO SEND TO ALL WOMEN!).<br /><br />I am obviously NOT the audience for these types of books. I think it's absolutely disgusting to romanticize an ABUSIVE STALKER. Ladies. A man forcing himself on you after you said no is BAD. I don't care how hot he is. He just FORCED HIMSELF ON YOU AFTER YOU SAID NO. THIS IS NOT SEXY. THIS IS NOT ROMANTIC. A man who keeps purposely showing up at places where you're going to be AFTER you've told him you're not interested is called a STALKER. This also is NOT romantic or sexy!<br /><br />What the fuck is wrong with people? Seriously?<br /><br /></span>

    <a title="Evgeny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9340136-evgeny"><img alt="Evgeny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1544797852p2/9340136.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3222035470?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Evgeny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Evgeny" href="/user/show/9340136-evgeny">Evgeny</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/41060893-in-flight">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Evgeny by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9340136-evgeny?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3222035470" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1499902450379244926">My two-line review follows. The bad: the book is practically a repeat of Fifty Shades. The good: it is better written. The end. <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1584118564i/29102270._SX540_.jpg' alt='Fifty Shades' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>My rumbling review. A flight attendant Bianca Karlsson (by the way if somebody asks me to name a typical Swedish last name, like Smith in English this would be my first answer) was obviously Swedish in origin, an orphan, and has countless number of personal demons to conquer. <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1584118503i/29102268._SX540_.jpg' alt='Bianca' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>To her defense the demons were not of her own making. She had a best friend Stephen who was luc</span>
  <span id="freeText1499902450379244926" style="display:none">My two-line review follows. The bad: the book is practically a repeat of Fifty Shades. The good: it is better written. The end. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1584118564i/29102270._SX540_.jpg" alt="Fifty Shades" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My rumbling review. A flight attendant Bianca Karlsson (by the way if somebody asks me to name a typical Swedish last name, like Smith in English this would be my first answer) was obviously Swedish in origin, an orphan, and has countless number of personal demons to conquer. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1584118503i/29102268._SX540_.jpg" alt="Bianca" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>To her defense the demons were not of her own making. She had a best friend Stephen who was luckily gay and thus an owner of an excellent crying shoulder for Bianca. Speaking about which, in my personal opinion their relationship was one-sides regardless of what was said about it: I have never seen Bianca doing anything nice for Stephen with him going out of his way to be there for her. <br><br>One flight Bianca caught an eye of a character the likes of which are dime a dozen in contemporary romances, but practically non-existent in real life: a young and outrageously handsome billionaire James Cavendish; the guy was in his early twenties. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1584118682i/29102294._SX540_.jpg" alt="James" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>People having even most vague clue about Fifty Shades can easily guess the rest of the story. James took Bianca's virginity, showed her joys of being submissive (by the way the BDSM scenes were surprisingly mild), but Bianca could not stay with him due to her demons, her past catching up, and just to keep the plot moving and to make it possible for a sequel to appear. Obviously the book ends with a cliffhanger which could have been easily avoided by two main characters having a talk to each other like grownups. <br><br>Having said all of the above I have only two major complaints: the obvious similarity to Fifty Shades and Bianca's - I would not call this stupidity - naiveté. As a character James had the moments I would not be proud of in his place, but he looks better than Bianca when it comes to mental abilities. The story - taking apart from its inspiration - is quite good and so are some characters, like aforementioned Stephen. <br><br>The final rating is <b>3.5 stars</b> rounded up for several reasons. One of them is that this was a book that showed that romance subgenre of a BDSM billionaire is here to stay and the success of Fifty Shades was not a lucky accident. Many thanks to Patty for suggesting me the book. After several years I finally got around to read it. <br><br>P.S. Unfortunately I looked into the next book and realized I will not continue the series. It was very predictable and described exactly what I thought would happen after finishing this one. It is a usual and expected situation where the sequel is not as good as the original. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440525576i/15987211._SX540_.jpg" alt="Sequel" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="1499902450379244926" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/457374762?book_show_action=true">Nov 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer457374762" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12606974537690341451"><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397860ra/768131.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><br/><b>"I'm going to ruin you. I"ll be your first, and I'll fuck you so thoroughly that I'll be your last, too. You won't want any other man after I've gotten my hands on you. Every last inch of you."</b><br/><br/>And so the story begins... The story of a 23 year old flight attendant named Bianca who encounters the extremely good looking and highly controlling billionaire Mr. James Cavendish in the first class section on one of her flights. They both immediately feel a very strong connection between them and des</span>
  <span id="freeText12606974537690341451" style="display:none"><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397860ra/768131.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><b>"I'm going to ruin you. I"ll be your first, and I'll fuck you so thoroughly that I'll be your last, too. You won't want any other man after I've gotten my hands on you. Every last inch of you."</b><br><br>And so the story begins... The story of a 23 year old flight attendant named Bianca who encounters the extremely good looking and highly controlling billionaire Mr. James Cavendish in the first class section on one of her flights. They both immediately feel a very strong connection between them and despite Bianca's reservations they begin a steamy hot love affair. After that, Bianca finds herself being swept away in the fascinating, frightening and exciting new world that James introduces to her. Along the way they each have to deal with the troubles from their past that keep haunting them. Especially Bianca has been through a lot when she was young but still she managed to keep strong and built up a life for herself, together with her best friend Stephan (whose character I absolutely loved by the way; their friendship reminded me of the one between Eva and Cary from the Crossfire series). <br><br><b>"Life hurts. As long as it doesn't kill us, we weather it."</b><br><br>James, our male lead character, is a very possesive, dominant and powerfull man but at the same time he's also very insecure and he's constantly making sure he doesn't do anything to upset Bianca's feelings. He wants to make sure she's enjoying their arrangement as much as she is.<br><br><b>"I would give just about anything to know what's behind that cool composure of yours. And I would kill to know what you're thinking," he whispered against my hair. "I'm so afraid I'll offend you beyond repair, and that you'll never let me know how. You'll just leave and never speak to me again. Would you do that?"</b><br><br>Yes, the storyline very much resembles the one of Fifty Shades and the Crossfire series. Was is very original? No. Did I enjoy reading it anaway? Yes! R.K. Lilley managed to write a very enjoyable story with a funny twist that captures your attention from the moment you start reading it untill the very end. I really liked her clear writing style and the fact that it took place in the refreshing world of aircrafts and flight attendants. I thoroughly enjoyed reading this book and will definitely read the next ones in the series as well!<br></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_981168921" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Penny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7463065-penny"><img alt="Penny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420145167p2/7463065.jpg" /></a>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/981168921?book_show_action=true">Jun 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Penny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Penny" href="/user/show/7463065-penny">Penny</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7463065-penny?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7463065-penny?shelf=bdsm">bdsm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7463065-penny?shelf=a-read-adult-romace">a-read-adult-romace</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer981168921" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5267268368116965747">I am sorry but <b><i>In Flight</i> didn’t work for me</b>.<br/><br/>I know many people loved this book, and that’s precisely why I gave it a go however, much to my disappointment, <b>it fell down</b> for me.<br/><br/>There are <b>several things wrongs with it</b>, here are just a few:<br/><br/>1)	There is seriously <b>something missing</b> here: <b>Depth</b>.<br/><br/>2)	<u>The Characters</u>:<br/> <b>I couldn’t connect</b> emotionally with the characters; as a result, I just didn’t care much about them. <br/><br/> <b>BIANCA</b> My biggest problem with her is that I don’t find her believable. I don’t see her b</span>
  <span id="freeText5267268368116965747" style="display:none">I am sorry but <b><i>In Flight</i> didn’t work for me</b>.<br /><br />I know many people loved this book, and that’s precisely why I gave it a go however, much to my disappointment, <b>it fell down</b> for me.<br /><br />There are <b>several things wrongs with it</b>, here are just a few:<br /><br />1)	There is seriously <b>something missing</b> here: <b>Depth</b>.<br /><br />2)	<u>The Characters</u>:<br /> <b>I couldn’t connect</b> emotionally with the characters; as a result, I just didn’t care much about them. <br /><br /> <b>BIANCA</b> My biggest problem with her is that I don’t find her believable. I don’t see her behavior coherent with her description. This happens often, an author tries to tell us who a character is but then fails to portrait that definition.<br />Another problem I have with her is <b>her trust in all matters James</b>. Leaving the sexual trust aside, there is something I cannot forgive her, the fact that she blindly believes James on <u>not using a condom</u> because she is on the pill, well, <b>that is messed up and utterly stupid</b>, she doesn’t really know him, how can she trust a complete stranger? How the hell does she know where he´s been, damn it? She doesn’t, they are not in any kind of relationship and not using a condom is unbelievably irresponsible and senile. Hello STDs!<br /><br /> <b>JAMES</b> He is a two-dimensional character, he absolutely lacks depth. James is a stranger. There is no way to connect to him and we really know nothing about him, except superficial facts. Even after the book ended he still felt like a stranger to me, distant, and I don’t mean in a mysterious kind of way, I mean in I have no idea who that guy is and I don’t even care way. He is incredibly flat. <br />Another problem I have with him is that sometimes when he talked I debated between gagging or wanting to punch him, maybe even both. Example: <i> “I’m going to tie you to my bed and take your hymen” </i> <b>WHAT.THE.FUCK. </b> Gag, punch and run the hell away!! Creep.<br /><br />3)	The way the sexual events unfold doesn’t seem realistic to me. It would have been different if the writer wouldn’t have decided to make Bianca a virgin, it would have make more sense if she wasn’t, but as it is, not so much. We have Bianca, a virgin, and in the scene where she looses her virginity that fact has to be not only told but also communicated throughout the scene, through the development of events. Well, that didn’t happen, I couldn’t believe it, it wasn’t realistic. She is a virgin, doesn’t date and on her VERY FIRST TIME she has NO PROBLEMS AT ALL accepting being tied up, dominated, using nipple claps and light BDSM stuff, she has <u>no doubts, not even a bit of fear, nervousness, or hesitation, nothing, NADA</u>, she just jumps right into it like a real pro. I would like to know WHERE DID <b>ALL THAT TRUST</b> TOWARDS JAMES CAME FROM, because there is nothing in the book up to that point to create that kind of connection and trust, she barely knows the dude, they haven’t even been on a date. I think that kind of confidence and trust doesn’t come so easily during your first time with someone you know, much less with an almost virtual stranger. The least we can expect is some <u>agitation</u>, anxiety or <u>nervousness</u>, hell some excitement at the minimum, the girl is completely inexperienced!<br /><br />I wanted to like it, I really did but <b><i>In flight</i> royally flunked</b>.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11508084990624973725"><b>5 Super Sexy Stars!</b><br/><br/>Going into reading this, I heard a lot about it being a mix of 50 Shades and Crossfire Series, and I do see the similarities. But move over Christian and Gideon... there is a new hot alpha in town that tops you both, my new book boyfriend....<br/><br/><i>Mr.Persistent, Mr.Stalker, Mr.Kinky, <b>Mr.Beautiful</b>, Mr.Dominant, Mr.Volatile, Mr.Shameless, Mr.Affectionate, Mr.Personality, Mr.Mercurial, Mr.Wonderful</i>,  <b>MR.CAVENDISH</b> <br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/chris%20hemsworth/kimasabe/1342726781.jpg?o=414' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <i>“I am going to ruin you,” he breathed. “I’ll be your first, and I’</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText11508084990624973725" style="display:none"><b>5 Super Sexy Stars!</b><br><br>Going into reading this, I heard a lot about it being a mix of 50 Shades and Crossfire Series, and I do see the similarities. But move over Christian and Gideon... there is a new hot alpha in town that tops you both, my new book boyfriend....<br><br><i>Mr.Persistent, Mr.Stalker, Mr.Kinky, <b>Mr.Beautiful</b>, Mr.Dominant, Mr.Volatile, Mr.Shameless, Mr.Affectionate, Mr.Personality, Mr.Mercurial, Mr.Wonderful</i>,  <b>MR.CAVENDISH</b> <br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/chris%20hemsworth/kimasabe/1342726781.jpg?o=414" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379783681i/448785.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>“I am going to ruin you,” he breathed. “I’ll be your first, and I’ll fuck you so thoroughly that I’ll be your last too. You won’t want any other man after I’ve gotten my hands on you.”</i>
</b> James... you are sooo yummy! <br><br>Now meet <b>Bianca</b> aka Buttercup, 23 year old flight attendant<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&amp;current=INFlightBianca.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398119i/769037.jpg" alt="Bianca IN FLIGHT" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Bianca is a flight attendant in the first class section. She and her best friend Stephan have worked in the field for a while and she is used to seeing the bigwigs, movie stars etc on her flights. But nothing prepares her for meeting billionaire businessman Mr. James Cavendish. There is something different about Mr. Cavendish. They have an insta-attraction to each other. James talks to Bianca about an arrangement of sorts, which she quickly declines. Bianca does not date. She is not interested... but there is something about Mr. Cavendish that wears her down. <br>Once they are together, the chemistry is undeniable! It is smoking hot! There are some steamy, passionate, straight up hot sex scenes, but this book is not all about the sex, there is actually a lot of story going on.<br><b>
  <i>“Life hurts. As long as it doesn’t kill us, we weather it.” </i>
</b><br>Both James and Bianca have traumatic and abusive pasts and are keeping some secrets from each other. Their pasts and issues cause there relationship to be complex. <br><br><b>James</b> is a hot dominate alpha male! Couldn’t get enough of him! He can be moody and controlling, but he is also affectionate, kind, sensitive and all kinds of sexy! <b>Bianca</b> has been through so much in her life, but she is still caring, smart, independent, and strong. She aggravated me at times, but knowing her past, you couldn’t be mad at her for the way she acted about some things. <b>Stephan</b> was one of my favorite characters! He reminded me of Carey from Bared to You, but better! Loved him!!! He was so much more than just a best friend to Bianca, he was her family. Loved their relationship and Stephan and James’ interactions. And no story would be complete without someone causing drama... Melissa and Jules- lets hope we don’t see too much of them in the next book! <br><br>Overall, In Flight was an amazing book! Some hot kink, memorable characters and a story with heart. Can’t wait to continue James and Bianca’s story and read Mile High. If you haven’t read this one, pick it up! It’s a must read! </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7444948037514852605"><b>3 SO-SO STARS</b><br/><br/>I'm on the fence with this book. It's not that I didn't like it but I didn't fall in love with it. It was like reading Fifty Shades for at least the first sixty percent of the book for me. I had a serious case of Déjà vu and lost complete interest. Sex wise, yes it was hot a</span>
  <span id="freeText7444948037514852605" style="display:none"><b>3 SO-SO STARS</b><br><br>I'm on the fence with this book. It's not that I didn't like it but I didn't fall in love with it. It was like reading Fifty Shades for at least the first sixty percent of the book for me. I had a serious case of Déjà vu and lost complete interest. It did at the end sort of begin to develop into something slightly different but I think that the character personalty traits were so similar to Christian and Ana's, that for me I had a hard time seeing past it. Sex wise, yes it was hot and steamy and I enjoyed that a lot but it lacked originality. I don't know. I don't really have much to say. I plan on reading book two but not anytime soon. The ending felt predictable to me and I wasn't left feeling like I had to have the second book immediately. <br><br> So......<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380371482ra/724557.gif" width="400" height="330" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Thats really all I have to say :/ <br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13877362801491095961"><b>Spoiler Free Review</b> <br/>3.5 to 4 STARS out of 5<br/>Genre: Adult Contemporary Romance -Erotica with BDSM<br/><b>Important Message:<br/>Shout Out to all Fifty Shades of Grey and Bared To You Fans.<i> THIS BOOK IS FOR YOU!</i> Kinky fuckery included.</b> <br/><br/><i>“I know it’s all consensual, but the fact is, I like to hurt women during sex.   There’s a reason you fear me.   My strongest impulse is to control and to dominate, but make no mistake, I’m a sadist.   It doesn’t exactly make me a good guy.”</i> ~James<br/><br/><b>Predator spots prey</b><br/>When first cl</span>
  <span id="freeText13877362801491095961" style="display:none"><b>Spoiler Free Review</b> <br />3.5 to 4 STARS out of 5<br />Genre: Adult Contemporary Romance -Erotica with BDSM<br /><b>Important Message:<br />Shout Out to all Fifty Shades of Grey and Bared To You Fans.<i> THIS BOOK IS FOR YOU!</i> Kinky fuckery included.</b> <br /><br /><i>“I know it’s all consensual, but the fact is, I like to hurt women during sex.   There’s a reason you fear me.   My strongest impulse is to control and to dominate, but make no mistake, I’m a sadist.   It doesn’t exactly make me a good guy.”</i> ~James<br /><br /><b>Predator spots prey</b><br />When first class flight attendant Bianca catches the piercing turquoise eyes of hotel billionaire James Cavendish her knees instantly go weak. Which really<b> really</b> sucks for her since she is trying to balance a tray of champagne filled glasses at 30,000 feet in the air. He watches her intensely for a good while. Once James finds out that the relationship between Bianca and Stephan her fellow flight attendant is strictly platonic...he goes in for the kill. <br />She tells James that she does not date, which is fine with him cause neither does he. James makes his intentions clear. He wants her, in his bed and at his mercy. Bianca turns him down of course.<br />And in true alpha male fashion James insinuates himself in to her life whether she wants him there or not.<br /> <br />The chemistry between these two was<i> HOT AS HELL</i>. The things they did on the plane was... Squirm inducing!<br /><br /><i>“That is the hottest fucking flight attendant uniform I’ve ever seen. That thing should be illegal. I’m going to do some illegal things to you with that little tease of a tie,”</i> ~James<br /><br /><b>James Cavendish</b> in one word <i>Delectable</i><br />It took me a while to get into this read because the real world kept interrupting my Caven<b>dish</b>. LOL!! Get it my Caven<b>dish</b>?! Ok, no... Not funny? Cool, moving on.<br /><br />I loved James he came across as a strong Dom yet would easily get thrown off balance by Bianca's nonchalant attitude. Which in my humble opinion just sucked him in more. In fact at times it was like he would walk on his tip toes afraid he would say something that would cause her to bolt.<br /><i><br />“You’re tying me in knots, yet you remain unaffected yourself. Are you just waiting for a reason to end this? That’s the impression I’m getting at the moment. And that drives me fucking crazy, since I don’t have a clue what will tip the scales against me.”</i> ~James<br /><br />This nonchalant attitude she gives frustrates him to no end because he desires to know her more yet she keeps him at arms length. But she does so with good reason. She believes that this is only an affair and will last weeks at the most. Her thoughts are clear, why complicate things by getting personal, lets keep it sexual.<br />After a while she caves and only agrees to give up personal information unless he does too! I give, you give becomes a routine that later leads them to both reveal painful secrets from their past. So painful that it brought tears to my eyes.<br /><br />PAUSE: The more I review this the more I realize how much I enjoyed it I will be changing this to a full 4 star rating now.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Welcome to the 4th floor, Bianca.”</i>
</b> ~James<br /> **Whispers** The 4th floor is the sex floor with his toys ;)<br /><br />These two definitely compliment each other on the<b> 'I am fucked up meter'</b> and at one point she voices how people like her need people like him. In other words hello masochist I would like you to meet my friend sadist.<br /><br /><i>“But I’m irrevocably fucked up, so you excite me in equal measures.   I find it liberating, to let someone control me. Someone who makes me tremble with fear. I’ve spent a great deal of my life running from the things that scare me, so this has been illuminating for me.”</i> ~Bianca<br /><br />The story takes a turn around the 82% mark. I continuously yelled<b> OH HELL NO</b>. James does something that royally pissed me off. Even after hearing why he did it I am still pissed. <br /> <br /><u>Thoughts</u><br />Overall I enjoyed it! I am huge Christian Grey and Gideon Cross fan. I felt this book stuck close to the "formula" some readers have grown to love me included.<br /><br /><b>The formula:</b> <br />-H/h both have traumatizing past that has left them with particular needs.<br />- The man is an all out alpha male<br />- The man is a billionaire<br />- The man has stalker tendencies<br />- The females have a great best friend that will defend them<br />- The females have no idea what they're getting in to with the male<br />- The females have emotional sobbing meltdowns<br />- Paparazzi play a small role<br />- The past creeps up to bite them in the ass<br /> Am I missing something?? Feel free to tell me I will gladly add it.<br /><br />My Rating<br />Characters- lovable, Intense and Damaged<br />Writing Style- Sexy, Emotional, Raw and Savory<br />Storyline/Plot- Good/Page turner<br />Steam Factor- High/Very Steamy<br />Overall- I enjoyed it!! Read it!<br /><b><br />Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!!</b></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer478656520" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer4725129937313024649">Re read February 2013 (couldn't stay away from a favourite)!<br/><br/>Mr Beautiful aka James Cavendish you have stolen my book heart, move over every other book hero, Mr Cavendish is here to stay as a firm favourite.<br/><br/>My first thoughts before starting this book was that it must be a rip off of similar books in this genre. How wrong was I?<br/><br/> This book had full content, great story telling and fabulous writing that went perfectly alongside the sexual nature and romance of the book. <br/><br/>The character development in </span>
  <span id="freeText4725129937313024649" style="display:none">Re read February 2013 (couldn't stay away from a favourite)!<br><br>Mr Beautiful aka James Cavendish you have stolen my book heart, move over every other book hero, Mr Cavendish is here to stay as a firm favourite.<br><br>My first thoughts before starting this book was that it must be a rip off of similar books in this genre. How wrong was I?<br><br> This book had full content, great story telling and fabulous writing that went perfectly alongside the sexual nature and romance of the book. <br><br>The character development in this book is surprisingly thorough. James our leading hero is such a likeable main character his dark past and flaws add a depth to his like-ability, I can not resist the domineering alpha male and Mr Cavendish delivers this role to perfection.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401018i/777642.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Girl crush alert - one lovely, feisty book heroine! Be prepared to love Bianca - the leading female character, strong, feisty and beautiful.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398083i/768928._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can't write my review without mentioning Stephan -Bianca's best friend a wonderfully written in sub character, his presence in the book provides Bianca with a support network, a character you can't help but want to get to know.<br><br>I was truly surprised by this well written enjoyable, seriously addictive story and as you can tell I'm now a firm fan, eagerly awaiting book two in the series. I would recommend to anyone who likes a book featuring good characters, an overly protective, dominant, but sweet main leading character with a female lead that needs to be loved away from her past. <br><br>I will recommend this to my fellow romance addicts, and happily stalk the author for future books.<br><br>4.5 Mr Cavendish stars, and a big craving for book two.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1313278083" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer16486845037380007787">I read the books last year but never left a review. I recently purchased the audio version for my long car rides to work so I thought I would review both the book and the audio.<br/><br/>This book series is my favorite series out of everything I have read. I keep thinking another series will come along and top this but that hasn't happened yet. The biggest reason I am so in love with this series is James and Bianca, the MC's. <br/><br/>I absolutely love James devotion to Bianca in this series. I tend to lean more t</span>
  <span id="freeText16486845037380007787" style="display:none">I read the books last year but never left a review. I recently purchased the audio version for my long car rides to work so I thought I would review both the book and the audio.<br /><br />This book series is my favorite series out of everything I have read. I keep thinking another series will come along and top this but that hasn't happened yet. The biggest reason I am so in love with this series is James and Bianca, the MC's. <br /><br />I absolutely love James devotion to Bianca in this series. I tend to lean more to the instant love, strong alpha stories and this has both. You don't realize how devoted James is in the beginning of this first book but it becomes pretty obvious the more you read. <br /><br />I'm a really big fan of Bianca's character as well. I don't particularly love it when authors have the females role chase the men, especially when they forgive too much with other women drama, so when I find a female character that demands respect, I'm thrilled. This series is a Dominant/Submissive series, however, the way RK Lilley wrote Bianca, she is a submissive but still expects to be treated respectfully. <br /><br />Bianca has not had good male role models in her life so she is very aloof with male attention. I like that James has to work for her affection. I'm not very educated on the BDSM lifestyle and I'm actually not that much of a fan. I prefer just a dominant male in my stories but the fact that this series has BDSM and I still love it just proves to me how really good this series is. <br /><br />Now for the audio review. I have just recently started listening to Audio books so I don't have too much reference to pull from but this is the third narrator I have listened too and she has been my favorite so far. In my other experience, I didn't really like the woman impersonating the male voices but this narrator did a much better job. She has also had to do 2 accents in this first book and I can't find fault in either accent. Really good job!<br /><br />If I could give this book more than 5 Stars, I would!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16486845037380007787" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1961956370535995707">-Why am I not rating this book?<br/><br/>Because I'm obviously not this book's audience. Like, at all. So rating it would be a bit unfair to the author and to the prospective readers.<br/><br/>-Why did you read it then?<br/><br/>I was curious and wanted to see what the fuss was all about.<br/><br/>-Did you find out what the fuss was about?<br/><br/>No.<br/><br/>-Did you like anything about it?<br/><br/>The writing was barebones and a bit dry, but not terrible.   <span id="freeText1961956370535995707" style="display:none">-Why am I not rating this book?<br /><br />Because I'm obviously not this book's audience. Like, at all. So rating it would be a bit unfair to the author and to the prospective readers.<br /><br />-Why did you read it then?<br /><br />I was curious and wanted to see what the fuss was all about.<br /><br />-Did you find out what the fuss was about?<br /><br />No.<br /><br />-Did you like anything about it?<br /><br />The writing was barebones and a bit dry, but not terrible. So that's a plus (really, quality writing is a dealbreaker for me, more than anything else). I actually didn't mind the heroine, Bianca. Her friend Stephen was a bright point. Being the daughter of a flight attendant, I appreciated how true to life Bianca's job was and I also liked that she was an artist.<br /><br />-What about the dude everyone loves?<br /><br />I don't really remember anything about him except he was very tan.<br /><br />-Who do you recommend this book to?<br /><br />Obviously anyone who liked 50 Shades of Grey. I think it's a huge step-up from it (again, Bianca ain't a bad heroine). And anyone who didn't like 50, but likes the whole billionaire and faux-BDSM thing (I don't like either, hence why I'm not the audience for the book) will most likely love this book. So there!<br /><br /> <br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_667322652" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/667322652" />
    <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga"><img alt="Beatrice Masaluñga" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603719912p2/4590441.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/667322652?book_show_action=true">Jul 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beatrice Masaluñga" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga">Beatrice Masaluñga</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga?shelf=adult">adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer667322652" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14020364357354832101">I like the author's writing style. It's easy to get into the story though I have slow moments on some parts. The romantic scenes are absolutely hot and well-written. However, I find this book a little cliché. It's like <i>Fifty Shades of Grey </i> and <i> Bared to You</i> mash-up. It's my pet peeve when guys are too possessive and stalker-ish even at work. James Cavendish is an example. Bianca is a flight stewardess, it's just ridiculous he makes a way to make sure she's safe. Nothing wrong on checking but ha</span>
  <span id="freeText14020364357354832101" style="display:none">I like the author's writing style. It's easy to get into the story though I have slow moments on some parts. The romantic scenes are absolutely hot and well-written. However, I find this book a little cliché. It's like <i>Fifty Shades of Grey </i> and <i> Bared to You</i> mash-up. It's my pet peeve when guys are too possessive and stalker-ish even at work. James Cavendish is an example. Bianca is a flight stewardess, it's just ridiculous he makes a way to make sure she's safe. Nothing wrong on checking but have someone to follow you around? Nope.<br /><br />I'm definitely continuing this and see the progress of the story. It's a good start. </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_459053163" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/459053163" />
    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/459053163?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=bdsm">bdsm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=steamy-reads">steamy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=rich-guy-hero">rich-guy-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer459053163" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16490508194180899173"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390689106i/8264770._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398116i/769023._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Unfortunately, for me, this was just a little <i>too</i> reminiscent of Fifty Shades, Bared To You, etc. <br/><br/>Hot billionaire sets sights on beautiful ordinary girl, said billionaire pursues girl relentlessly, both have tales of harrowing pasts, nightmares, insecurities, throw a token best gay/male friend, a chauffeur driven SUV, guys hired to follow the girl around and a secret love of BSM that's been hidden from the media, oh and of course 'the other woman', and you've got yourself a pretty standard found</span>
  <span id="freeText16490508194180899173" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390689106i/8264770._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398116i/769023._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Unfortunately, for me, this was just a little <i>too</i> reminiscent of Fifty Shades, Bared To You, etc. <br><br>Hot billionaire sets sights on beautiful ordinary girl, said billionaire pursues girl relentlessly, both have tales of harrowing pasts, nightmares, insecurities, throw a token best gay/male friend, a chauffeur driven SUV, guys hired to follow the girl around and a secret love of BSM that's been hidden from the media, oh and of course 'the other woman', and you've got yourself a pretty standard foundation for another erotic trilogy.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>He lay down beside me, pulling me back to his chest and throwing his arm over me. “Mine,” he whispered in my ear.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Sound familiar?<br><br>Don't get me wrong, I love a hot billionaire (who doesn't, right?) and I love 50 Shades <i>and</i> the Crossfire trilogy... but I also like a bit of variety and expect some imagination from an author.<br><br>For that, I've knocked off a star... but I could only force myself to knock off just the one. I did enjoy the book and it was super hot, so I didn't want to be too harsh!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Even mosochists need lovers. What would a girl like me do without someone like you? Perhaps everyone is good for someone."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Some of the sex scenes, holy christ, they were scorching! James Cavendish knows his shit. I loved his two personalities, the tender lover and the bossy dom. All hail Mr. Beautiful!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I’m going to ruin you. I’ll be your first, and I’ll fuck you so thoroughly that I’ll be your last too. You won’t want any other man after I’ve gotten my hands on you.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>So there we go. If you fancy a bit of steam and don't mind the blindingly obvious similarities to a certain few favourite sexy trilogies, give In Flight a whirl. I will be reading the rest of the trilogy... probably... just not yet, I need something unique to get my teeth into next.<br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16490508194180899173" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
