<div id="review_458883784" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/458883784" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/458883784?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-book-1">series-book-1</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=billionaire">billionaire</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer458883784" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14752370484176440527"><b>I LOOOOOOOOVE THIS BOOK!!!</b><br/><br/>I started it wanting to get swept away in an intense, emotional love story, and that’s exactly what I got. Yes, it’s similar to Fifty Shades, and the Crossfire books, but I love those, so I figure what’s wrong with adding one more to the pile of dominant, controlling and sexy-as-hell billionaires? It’s all good!<br/><br/>Having said that though, I’m glad I waited until I was in just the right mood to read it. Otherwise I probably would have been amongst those readers who wrote it</span>
  <span id="freeText14752370484176440527" style="display:none"><b>I LOOOOOOOOVE THIS BOOK!!!</b><br><br>I started it wanting to get swept away in an intense, emotional love story, and that’s exactly what I got. Yes, it’s similar to Fifty Shades, and the Crossfire books, but I love those, so I figure what’s wrong with adding one more to the pile of dominant, controlling and sexy-as-hell billionaires? It’s all good!<br><br>Having said that though, I’m glad I waited until I was in just the right mood to read it. Otherwise I probably would have been amongst those readers who wrote it off as too similar to other books out there. <br><br>James and Bianca’s story had me sucked in from the very first page. Their sizzling attraction to each other is evident from their first meeting, where Bianca is the flight attendant in the first class cabin where billionaire Executive James is seated. There is some intense eye fuckery between them, and James immediately begins his relentless pursuit. Promising her things beyond her comprehension, it doesn’t take James long to coax innocent Bianca into his world.<br><br><i>“I’m not into any of that stuff, so we are clearly not compatible.”<br>He ran a long finger down his own tie the way he had done to mine. “I’m not sure if that one was a lie or if you just don’t know how pleasurable ‘that stuff’ can be. Or how well suited you are to it. I can show you. I would love to show you. When I’m done with you, I’ll know your body better than you do, and you will be begging me for it. Every inch of your body is submitting to me, even as you’re turning me down. Can you honestly tell me that the thought of submitting to me in bed doesn’t make you wet?”</i><br><br>Yeah, he’s not exactly shy!!! But he is respectful and considerate, and he never pushes Bianca into something she’s not ready for. And when they do get together… HOT DAMN!!! There are some <u>serious</u> fireworks!!! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Although I do need to question James’ apparent superpower of saying the word “come” and Bianca going off on command… every single freaking time. What is that about? Weird! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>But behind the hot and steamy sex, and the developing romance between the two of them, they both have nastiness in their past. Bianca, in particular, is still dealing with a tragedy in her childhood that continues to haunt her. She is cynical and untrusting and doesn’t quite know how to deal when James comes crashing into her life. <br><br><i>“You scare me … But I’m irrevocably fucked up, so you excite me in equal measures.”</i><br><br>She acts unaffected and plays games with him. Convinced that he’s just using her, she keeps herself closed off from him, and is determined not to get too deeply involved, always looking for some sort of sign from him that shows that he’s going to leave her - therefore justifying her keeping him at arm’s length. It’s annoying, but understandable once you learn her backstory.<br><br>And can I just say - <u>I freaking love James Cavendish!!!!</u> He’s quite the contradiction! Hot and dirty, but also incredibly tender - being patient with Bianca while she comes to terms with all of the things he is introducing her to, and caring for her so beautifully. Yes, he is dominant and controlling, but he is always respectful of her and at times, is also quite vulnerable. Bianca’s behaviour drives him (and me) crazy, since he has no clue what the trigger will be that will make her want to run. And watching him trying to make her feel safe, and get her to open up to him was just gorgeous!<br><br>Their relationship is very intense from the beginning but, as I discussed with a friend, we all know that obsessive, controlling, instantly-in-love men may be creepy and weird in the real world, but in fiction land, they are the best… AND WE LOVE IT! There are dramas and fights, heaps of steaminess – which thankfully never overshadows the actual story - lots of tender and swoony moments, and an ending that has me clamouring to get my hands on the next book in the series. <br><br>Huge shout out to Stephan for being one of the most incredible best friends EVER! He is protective, supportive, funny, and the bond that he and Bianca have is amazing! I loved how they are there for each other, no matter what, no questions asked. They share each other's lives, and I loved how he encourages Bianca to take a chance on James, and supports their relationship all the way. <i>"Somebody is smitten with my Buttercup"</i> Perfect!<br><br>With just the right mix of drama, emotion, swoon and sex appeal, I was completely swept away by this story, and am going straight on to book 2.<br><br>4.5 stars :)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398090i/768958._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>* * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * * *<br><br><br>Below are the reviews for the extras that are available...<br><br>Finally! A glimpse into the mind of James Cavendish! This is a very quick little short - the scene is the second time that James is on Bianca's flight and he makes his (very unsubtle) move. Hot! I love seeing the intensity behind his motivation. <br><br>Loved it.<br><br><br><br>Another peek inside the mind of obsessive, possessive James Cavendish. <br><br>Again, seeing as this scene happens so early in book 1, we get to marvel at just how smitten James is with Bianca from the very beginning. <br><br>"I'm in trouble with this one, <i>I thought. For the first time in my life, I had the thought that I was in over my head with a woman.<br>She started singing and giggling in her soft voice and my brain did a little short circuiting. </i>Fuck, I'm in trouble." <br><br>I'm already a Stephan fan, and loved how he was James' side from the very beginning, but seeing him lay it out for him was awesome. <br><br>"<i>If you don't treat her well, I will hurt you. I don't care how rich you are, I will kick your ass."<br>He said it as though he honestly couldn't help it. <br>I nodded at him to show him that I understood. "I want you to trust me Stephan. As I said, I want to take care of her. I swear to you that I'll treat her like a Princess</i>" <br><br>... a Princess with a fetish for kink... but that's a whole nother story ;)<br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="14752370484176440527" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14424337404921204516">2.5 <br/>Maybe intrigued enough to read the next book, but really I started this series just to get to the Tristan and Danika series. This is just so cliche billionaire BDSM, it's not even funny. The thing that makes it stand out a bit is the fact that the heroine truly is not looking for a relationship, and the hero eventually crawls. I liked that part :D</span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('OZ3a6BdGFtLlr/p4xr0tjhYzPjJVgntw5J3CMHA4yk6CknAdFT0gyb43AWpwCPW1Ncg4c5Rd2peT8sw1Y1KoWw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('0+FrTWGFZGvWpp8NJ+T36m7c7S2xKivS90iB+d5KZP9o7sG4Y/5ScI0+ZB+RUS/RTSfrbHD1ijWAJ4/8zSAG6g==')})
  }
//]]>

For several years she was a first class flight attendant, and she always swore that she just had to write a book about it. Mixing her love of romance and all things BDSM, the Up In the Air Trilogy is her debut into the world of contempary romance and erotica. She is currently working on </span>
